## Projects

### Architecture

_Frameworks and libraries that help implementing and verifying design and architecture concepts._

<!-- SECTION:Architecture -->
<table style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;border-collapse:collapse;">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/TNG/ArchUnit">ArchUnit</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Test library for specifying and asserting architecture rules.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TNG/ArchUnit?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/TNG/ArchUnit?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/xmolecules/jmolecules">jMolecules</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Annotations and interfaces to express design and architecture concepts in code.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xmolecules/jmolecules?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/xmolecules/jmolecules?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Artificial Intelligence

_Frameworks that help you to leverage LLMs and AI._



<!-- SECTION:Artificial Intelligence -->
<table style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;border-collapse:collapse;">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/langchain4j/langchain4j">LangChain4j</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Simplifies integration of LLMs with unified APIs and a comprehensive toolbox.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/langchain4j/langchain4j?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/langchain4j/langchain4j?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/java-sdk">MCP Java SDK</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Enables applications to interact with AI models and tools through a standardized interface (i.e. Model Context Protocol), supporting both synchronous and asynchronous communication patterns.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/modelcontextprotocol/java-sdk?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/modelcontextprotocol/java-sdk?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/sashirestela/simple-openai">simple-openai</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Library to use the OpenAI API (and compatible ones) in the simplest possible way.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sashirestela/simple-openai?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sashirestela/simple-openai?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://spring.io/projects/spring-ai">Spring AI</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Application framework for AI engineering for Spring.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Bean Mapping

_Frameworks that ease bean mapping._



<!-- SECTION:Bean Mapping -->
<table style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;border-collapse:collapse;">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/doov-io/doov">dOOv</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Provides fluent API for typesafe domain model validation and mapping. It uses annotations, code generation and a type safe DSL to make bean validation and mapping fast and easy.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/doov-io/doov?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/doov-io/doov?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/jmapper-framework/jmapper-core">JMapper</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Uses byte code manipulation for lightning-fast mapping. Supports annotations and API or XML configuration.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jmapper-framework/jmapper-core?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/jmapper-framework/jmapper-core?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/mapstruct/mapstruct">MapStruct</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Code generator that simplifies mappings between different bean types, based on a convention-over-configuration approach.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mapstruct/mapstruct?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/mapstruct/mapstruct?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/modelmapper/modelmapper">ModelMapper</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Intelligent object mapping library that automatically maps objects to each other.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/modelmapper/modelmapper?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/modelmapper/modelmapper?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/orika-mapper/orika">Orika</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">JavaBean-mapping framework that recursively copies (among other capabilities) data from one object to another.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orika-mapper/orika?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/orika-mapper/orika?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/remondis-it/remap">reMap</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Lambda and method handle-based mapping which requires code and not annotations if objects have different names.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/remondis-it/remap?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/remondis-it/remap?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/xebia-france/selma">Selma</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Annotation processor-based bean mapper.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xebia-france/selma?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/xebia-france/selma?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Build

_Tools that handle the build cycle and dependencies of an application._



<!-- SECTION:Build -->
<table style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;border-collapse:collapse;">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://maven.apache.org">Apache Maven</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Declarative build and dependency management that favors convention over configuration. It might be preferable to Apache Ant, which uses a rather procedural approach and can be difficult to maintain.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://bazel.build">Bazel</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Tool from Google that builds code quickly and reliably.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/facebook/buck2">Buck2</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Encourages the creation of small, reusable modules consisting of code and resources.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/buck2?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/facebook/buck2?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://gradle.org">Gradle</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Incremental builds programmed via Groovy instead of declaring XML. Works well with Maven's dependency management.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Bytecode Manipulation

_Libraries to manipulate bytecode programmatically._



<!-- SECTION:Bytecode Manipulation -->
<table style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;border-collapse:collapse;">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://asm.ow2.io">ASM</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">All-purpose, low-level bytecode manipulation and analysis.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://bytebuddy.net">Byte Buddy</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Further simplifies bytecode generation with a fluent API.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/Konloch/bytecode-viewer">bytecode-viewer</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Java 8 Jar & Android APK reverse engineering suite. (GPL-3.0-only)</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Konloch/bytecode-viewer?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Konloch/bytecode-viewer?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://byteman.jboss.org">Byteman</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Manipulate bytecode at runtime via DSL (rules); mainly for testing/troubleshooting. (LGPL-2.1-or-later)</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/cglib/cglib">cglib</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Bytecode generation library.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cglib/cglib?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/cglib/cglib?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/jboss-javassist/javassist">Javassist</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Tries to simplify bytecode editing.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jboss-javassist/javassist?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/jboss-javassist/javassist?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/cojen/maker">Maker</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Provides low level bytecode generation.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cojen/maker?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/cojen/maker?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/SpongePowered/Mixin">Mixin</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Manipulate bytecode at runtime using real Java code.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SpongePowered/Mixin?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/SpongePowered/Mixin?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://github.com/nicolasmanic/perses">Perses</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Dynamically injects failure/latency at the bytecode level according to principles of chaos engineering.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nicolasmanic/perses?style=flat-square&label=" alt="GitHub stars"></td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;"><img src="https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nicolasmanic/perses?style=flat-square&label=" alt="Last commit"></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://www.coley.software/Recaf/">Recaf</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">JVM reverse engineering toolkit, essentially an IDE for Java bytecode.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

    </tr>

      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://infinispan.org">Infinispan</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Highly concurrent key/value datastore used for caching.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>

### CLI

_Libraries for everything related to the CLI._

#### Argument Parsing

_Libraries to assist with parsing command line arguments._



<!-- SECTION:CLI > Argument Parsing -->
<table style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;border-collapse:collapse;">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="https://rvesse.github.io/airline/">Airline</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Annotation-based framework for parsing Git-like command-line arguments.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">
        <a href="http://jcommander.org">JCommander</a>
      </td>
      <td style="width:65%;word-wrap:break-word;">Command-line argument-parsing framework with custom types and validation via implementing interfaces.</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
      <td style="width:7.5%;text-align:center;">-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="width:20%;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">

### Influential Books

_Books that made a big impact and are still worth reading._

- [Core Java Volume I--Fundamentals](https://www.amazon.com/Core-Java-I-Fundamentals-10th/dp/0134177304)
- [Core Java, Volume II--Advanced Features](https://www.amazon.com/Core-Java-II-Advanced-Features-10th/dp/0134177290)
- [Effective Java (3rd Edition)](https://www.amazon.com/Effective-Java-3rd-Joshua-Bloch/dp/0134685997)
- [Head First Java (3rd Edition)](https://www.oreilly.com/library/view/head-first-java/9781492091646/)
- [Java Concurrency in Practice](https://www.amazon.com/Java-Concurrency-Practice-Brian-Goetz/dp/0321349601)
- [The Well-Grounded Java Developer (2nd Edition)](https://www.manning.com/books/the-well-grounded-java-developer-second-edition)
- [Thinking in Java](https://www.amazon.com/Thinking-Java-Edition-Bruce-Eckel/dp/0131872486)
